# 3-13 MHA-master high availability 

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/ba60f547-c67b-4fbe-960e-aa515f57a3cf/SCR-20240729-nfef.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RBW2QQVM%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231213Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCICgAwAXbj1gh8jyHKgjjJ%2FLYX2mdCEEEo8716DiTNwK8AiBQfVlY4738ISFpguGSkhKIv4mu%2BAU%2Fy05sOw4YBZ0KzyqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIMf9y6Q3pH7MoB%2BnggKtwDoMndApzs2fqpLlt2EHgT0maf%2FZTFGogO3Hv44KZ1bi2%2Fs5XeAYoXfrcF0gAwketkIC5nNXyIMVNBuvp79pDL0squcyS74h49A3ucqYDqLZVDwzqr3WxG1TdxdetcPzcdH5EtC13j1Zcn7N0kgYKGt7EDyNrJA1LqUsDOnv9%2BZpvqGVNaCSoeJaPhvhgoo4zPst%2FyRSb16czls7pv1Z7pl24e9D4odvzdFrLR0cqtPP8vmobsWwya1W%2BoYd25SCa0iPuzeMdYp5m2u5fKNmKLN%2FCVf7O%2BCNTKua7yCysqCmgEBeoZ8qGnMVGAoTC3Zhbd6Ws3ygc%2F4TTNoDNf5qqSCF7Wtrm3d%2FO3eyfTevWcprM1RLiK5451Bba99HloSouzAbFyPusOMEuQYDx5%2Bs9kMZSMQEN7qXCHrXx3ezODfP0H%2FY7jtyUaBFUF1DMWA%2BMbf9lTUGBVT%2FwWVygxQtOuEIc88spnABaKf1VBZlQYSmFtQRTobTglIGqK4%2BuxaWX8xeKGB%2F4zTi%2BqzgXwN%2BTFrdigohLSI%2BQo6qAcowtXsoiSufIPeD5lgaf22q1ZAKZDISWc1Uk2CqqTyZVDa%2Fy3dz%2BL8X3T8sljdIe61mmeb9Q9%2FnEOEi0rm4X67iMw2rf%2F0gY6pgHpc0v%2FtRxZH%2B9yUignjKSwFTPxF9YYTBXHBCfLrG3FXgC2w4rF4KfYTIQg2yb1r5E9DEmdJiJETR%2BNvRIOSmFWH2A1KfcyDzI8NIFcblFS%2BHz6oJVyl7uj%2FyFB6pNXXCMG1NE0CDUa18dlqZnVYHS8wTIzf8IhVsNHahYxM9yOWRUutrSy62coWyJtL%2Flm6Ya5uDx14H3fT9irNqryIQw7KQKLOeRT&X-Amz-Signature=e748b59f1128133829bb4d6057fe8474714d8554a0e125a94465a2e95b8fad28&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

大家好，我是大木。这节课来探讨 MHA。 MHA 是 master high availability 的简称。这是一个日本工程师基于 perl 脚本语言编写的一个 MySQL 管理工具。它能在主从复制的基础上实现主节点的自动故障转移。自动故障转移的时间一般在 30 秒以内，还是非常迅速的。简单来说， MHA 它是一套比较优秀的 MySQL 高可用解决方案。 

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/9165d68b-3278-4faa-b7fa-19806502f92f/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RBW2QQVM%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231213Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCICgAwAXbj1gh8jyHKgjjJ%2FLYX2mdCEEEo8716DiTNwK8AiBQfVlY4738ISFpguGSkhKIv4mu%2BAU%2Fy05sOw4YBZ0KzyqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIMf9y6Q3pH7MoB%2BnggKtwDoMndApzs2fqpLlt2EHgT0maf%2FZTFGogO3Hv44KZ1bi2%2Fs5XeAYoXfrcF0gAwketkIC5nNXyIMVNBuvp79pDL0squcyS74h49A3ucqYDqLZVDwzqr3WxG1TdxdetcPzcdH5EtC13j1Zcn7N0kgYKGt7EDyNrJA1LqUsDOnv9%2BZpvqGVNaCSoeJaPhvhgoo4zPst%2FyRSb16czls7pv1Z7pl24e9D4odvzdFrLR0cqtPP8vmobsWwya1W%2BoYd25SCa0iPuzeMdYp5m2u5fKNmKLN%2FCVf7O%2BCNTKua7yCysqCmgEBeoZ8qGnMVGAoTC3Zhbd6Ws3ygc%2F4TTNoDNf5qqSCF7Wtrm3d%2FO3eyfTevWcprM1RLiK5451Bba99HloSouzAbFyPusOMEuQYDx5%2Bs9kMZSMQEN7qXCHrXx3ezODfP0H%2FY7jtyUaBFUF1DMWA%2BMbf9lTUGBVT%2FwWVygxQtOuEIc88spnABaKf1VBZlQYSmFtQRTobTglIGqK4%2BuxaWX8xeKGB%2F4zTi%2BqzgXwN%2BTFrdigohLSI%2BQo6qAcowtXsoiSufIPeD5lgaf22q1ZAKZDISWc1Uk2CqqTyZVDa%2Fy3dz%2BL8X3T8sljdIe61mmeb9Q9%2FnEOEi0rm4X67iMw2rf%2F0gY6pgHpc0v%2FtRxZH%2B9yUignjKSwFTPxF9YYTBXHBCfLrG3FXgC2w4rF4KfYTIQg2yb1r5E9DEmdJiJETR%2BNvRIOSmFWH2A1KfcyDzI8NIFcblFS%2BHz6oJVyl7uj%2FyFB6pNXXCMG1NE0CDUa18dlqZnVYHS8wTIzf8IhVsNHahYxM9yOWRUutrSy62coWyJtL%2Flm6Ya5uDx14H3fT9irNqryIQw7KQKLOeRT&X-Amz-Signature=25c22b247a9cff04a68d9e7dc307530de0a674583689ab7aa1c9b178a17f2071&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

github 地址在这里，感兴趣的同学可以看一看。


下面来看一下 MHA 的原理。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/22b00ae3-da1e-4fd4-bdbf-e0fd9903cd12/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RBW2QQVM%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231213Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCICgAwAXbj1gh8jyHKgjjJ%2FLYX2mdCEEEo8716DiTNwK8AiBQfVlY4738ISFpguGSkhKIv4mu%2BAU%2Fy05sOw4YBZ0KzyqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIMf9y6Q3pH7MoB%2BnggKtwDoMndApzs2fqpLlt2EHgT0maf%2FZTFGogO3Hv44KZ1bi2%2Fs5XeAYoXfrcF0gAwketkIC5nNXyIMVNBuvp79pDL0squcyS74h49A3ucqYDqLZVDwzqr3WxG1TdxdetcPzcdH5EtC13j1Zcn7N0kgYKGt7EDyNrJA1LqUsDOnv9%2BZpvqGVNaCSoeJaPhvhgoo4zPst%2FyRSb16czls7pv1Z7pl24e9D4odvzdFrLR0cqtPP8vmobsWwya1W%2BoYd25SCa0iPuzeMdYp5m2u5fKNmKLN%2FCVf7O%2BCNTKua7yCysqCmgEBeoZ8qGnMVGAoTC3Zhbd6Ws3ygc%2F4TTNoDNf5qqSCF7Wtrm3d%2FO3eyfTevWcprM1RLiK5451Bba99HloSouzAbFyPusOMEuQYDx5%2Bs9kMZSMQEN7qXCHrXx3ezODfP0H%2FY7jtyUaBFUF1DMWA%2BMbf9lTUGBVT%2FwWVygxQtOuEIc88spnABaKf1VBZlQYSmFtQRTobTglIGqK4%2BuxaWX8xeKGB%2F4zTi%2BqzgXwN%2BTFrdigohLSI%2BQo6qAcowtXsoiSufIPeD5lgaf22q1ZAKZDISWc1Uk2CqqTyZVDa%2Fy3dz%2BL8X3T8sljdIe61mmeb9Q9%2FnEOEi0rm4X67iMw2rf%2F0gY6pgHpc0v%2FtRxZH%2B9yUignjKSwFTPxF9YYTBXHBCfLrG3FXgC2w4rF4KfYTIQg2yb1r5E9DEmdJiJETR%2BNvRIOSmFWH2A1KfcyDzI8NIFcblFS%2BHz6oJVyl7uj%2FyFB6pNXXCMG1NE0CDUa18dlqZnVYHS8wTIzf8IhVsNHahYxM9yOWRUutrSy62coWyJtL%2Flm6Ya5uDx14H3fT9irNqryIQw7KQKLOeRT&X-Amz-Signature=e8fdba999f53ede40086ac85a3c14d159c938cc8b9debc3276c6de8c64873a1b&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

从图里面可以看到 MHA 它由两部分组成，一是 MHA manager，二是 MHA node。其中 manager 是 MHA 的管理工具，可以部署在一立的服务器上，用了管理多个 MySQL 主从复制。比方图里面一个 manager 可以管理两套主从复制, 当让了 manager 也可以不独立部署，比方部署到某一台从界点上 version 的环境。建议还是独立部署，这样职责比较分明一些，同时也不会影响从节点的服务质量。而 node 则是 MHA 的数据节点工具，每台数据库服务器都需要部署。


MHA 的功能主要

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/6ae87e84-7116-4f78-9942-541f3f1b8965/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RBW2QQVM%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231213Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCICgAwAXbj1gh8jyHKgjjJ%2FLYX2mdCEEEo8716DiTNwK8AiBQfVlY4738ISFpguGSkhKIv4mu%2BAU%2Fy05sOw4YBZ0KzyqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIMf9y6Q3pH7MoB%2BnggKtwDoMndApzs2fqpLlt2EHgT0maf%2FZTFGogO3Hv44KZ1bi2%2Fs5XeAYoXfrcF0gAwketkIC5nNXyIMVNBuvp79pDL0squcyS74h49A3ucqYDqLZVDwzqr3WxG1TdxdetcPzcdH5EtC13j1Zcn7N0kgYKGt7EDyNrJA1LqUsDOnv9%2BZpvqGVNaCSoeJaPhvhgoo4zPst%2FyRSb16czls7pv1Z7pl24e9D4odvzdFrLR0cqtPP8vmobsWwya1W%2BoYd25SCa0iPuzeMdYp5m2u5fKNmKLN%2FCVf7O%2BCNTKua7yCysqCmgEBeoZ8qGnMVGAoTC3Zhbd6Ws3ygc%2F4TTNoDNf5qqSCF7Wtrm3d%2FO3eyfTevWcprM1RLiK5451Bba99HloSouzAbFyPusOMEuQYDx5%2Bs9kMZSMQEN7qXCHrXx3ezODfP0H%2FY7jtyUaBFUF1DMWA%2BMbf9lTUGBVT%2FwWVygxQtOuEIc88spnABaKf1VBZlQYSmFtQRTobTglIGqK4%2BuxaWX8xeKGB%2F4zTi%2BqzgXwN%2BTFrdigohLSI%2BQo6qAcowtXsoiSufIPeD5lgaf22q1ZAKZDISWc1Uk2CqqTyZVDa%2Fy3dz%2BL8X3T8sljdIe61mmeb9Q9%2FnEOEi0rm4X67iMw2rf%2F0gY6pgHpc0v%2FtRxZH%2B9yUignjKSwFTPxF9YYTBXHBCfLrG3FXgC2w4rF4KfYTIQg2yb1r5E9DEmdJiJETR%2BNvRIOSmFWH2A1KfcyDzI8NIFcblFS%2BHz6oJVyl7uj%2FyFB6pNXXCMG1NE0CDUa18dlqZnVYHS8wTIzf8IhVsNHahYxM9yOWRUutrSy62coWyJtL%2Flm6Ya5uDx14H3fT9irNqryIQw7KQKLOeRT&X-Amz-Signature=491909e15a1af6aba7f61d872dd22d46c1ce1b226e10ab678e9de2736ee268d0&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

有三点一是故障自动切换，二是保证故障切换的过程中数据丢失尽可能小，三是保证故障切换之后，其他从库和新的主库数据是一致的。它是怎么实现的？

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/274b95d7-15a7-4bc3-a86c-f5270f324965/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RBW2QQVM%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231213Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCICgAwAXbj1gh8jyHKgjjJ%2FLYX2mdCEEEo8716DiTNwK8AiBQfVlY4738ISFpguGSkhKIv4mu%2BAU%2Fy05sOw4YBZ0KzyqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIMf9y6Q3pH7MoB%2BnggKtwDoMndApzs2fqpLlt2EHgT0maf%2FZTFGogO3Hv44KZ1bi2%2Fs5XeAYoXfrcF0gAwketkIC5nNXyIMVNBuvp79pDL0squcyS74h49A3ucqYDqLZVDwzqr3WxG1TdxdetcPzcdH5EtC13j1Zcn7N0kgYKGt7EDyNrJA1LqUsDOnv9%2BZpvqGVNaCSoeJaPhvhgoo4zPst%2FyRSb16czls7pv1Z7pl24e9D4odvzdFrLR0cqtPP8vmobsWwya1W%2BoYd25SCa0iPuzeMdYp5m2u5fKNmKLN%2FCVf7O%2BCNTKua7yCysqCmgEBeoZ8qGnMVGAoTC3Zhbd6Ws3ygc%2F4TTNoDNf5qqSCF7Wtrm3d%2FO3eyfTevWcprM1RLiK5451Bba99HloSouzAbFyPusOMEuQYDx5%2Bs9kMZSMQEN7qXCHrXx3ezODfP0H%2FY7jtyUaBFUF1DMWA%2BMbf9lTUGBVT%2FwWVygxQtOuEIc88spnABaKf1VBZlQYSmFtQRTobTglIGqK4%2BuxaWX8xeKGB%2F4zTi%2BqzgXwN%2BTFrdigohLSI%2BQo6qAcowtXsoiSufIPeD5lgaf22q1ZAKZDISWc1Uk2CqqTyZVDa%2Fy3dz%2BL8X3T8sljdIe61mmeb9Q9%2FnEOEi0rm4X67iMw2rf%2F0gY6pgHpc0v%2FtRxZH%2B9yUignjKSwFTPxF9YYTBXHBCfLrG3FXgC2w4rF4KfYTIQg2yb1r5E9DEmdJiJETR%2BNvRIOSmFWH2A1KfcyDzI8NIFcblFS%2BHz6oJVyl7uj%2FyFB6pNXXCMG1NE0CDUa18dlqZnVYHS8wTIzf8IhVsNHahYxM9yOWRUutrSy62coWyJtL%2Flm6Ya5uDx14H3fT9irNqryIQw7KQKLOeRT&X-Amz-Signature=cdafb969345b88e304045841c9863a9e5e4261abc90884b7f8cdcbbe8d78ef98&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

这么玩儿的？如果宕机的主库依然可以通过 ssh 连接，那么 MHA 会把宕机主库的 Binlog 保存起来，一会儿有用。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/159f1b33-52b4-4777-9d37-11aba77adeef/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RBW2QQVM%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231213Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCICgAwAXbj1gh8jyHKgjjJ%2FLYX2mdCEEEo8716DiTNwK8AiBQfVlY4738ISFpguGSkhKIv4mu%2BAU%2Fy05sOw4YBZ0KzyqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIMf9y6Q3pH7MoB%2BnggKtwDoMndApzs2fqpLlt2EHgT0maf%2FZTFGogO3Hv44KZ1bi2%2Fs5XeAYoXfrcF0gAwketkIC5nNXyIMVNBuvp79pDL0squcyS74h49A3ucqYDqLZVDwzqr3WxG1TdxdetcPzcdH5EtC13j1Zcn7N0kgYKGt7EDyNrJA1LqUsDOnv9%2BZpvqGVNaCSoeJaPhvhgoo4zPst%2FyRSb16czls7pv1Z7pl24e9D4odvzdFrLR0cqtPP8vmobsWwya1W%2BoYd25SCa0iPuzeMdYp5m2u5fKNmKLN%2FCVf7O%2BCNTKua7yCysqCmgEBeoZ8qGnMVGAoTC3Zhbd6Ws3ygc%2F4TTNoDNf5qqSCF7Wtrm3d%2FO3eyfTevWcprM1RLiK5451Bba99HloSouzAbFyPusOMEuQYDx5%2Bs9kMZSMQEN7qXCHrXx3ezODfP0H%2FY7jtyUaBFUF1DMWA%2BMbf9lTUGBVT%2FwWVygxQtOuEIc88spnABaKf1VBZlQYSmFtQRTobTglIGqK4%2BuxaWX8xeKGB%2F4zTi%2BqzgXwN%2BTFrdigohLSI%2BQo6qAcowtXsoiSufIPeD5lgaf22q1ZAKZDISWc1Uk2CqqTyZVDa%2Fy3dz%2BL8X3T8sljdIe61mmeb9Q9%2FnEOEi0rm4X67iMw2rf%2F0gY6pgHpc0v%2FtRxZH%2B9yUignjKSwFTPxF9YYTBXHBCfLrG3FXgC2w4rF4KfYTIQg2yb1r5E9DEmdJiJETR%2BNvRIOSmFWH2A1KfcyDzI8NIFcblFS%2BHz6oJVyl7uj%2FyFB6pNXXCMG1NE0CDUa18dlqZnVYHS8wTIzf8IhVsNHahYxM9yOWRUutrSy62coWyJtL%2Flm6Ya5uDx14H3fT9irNqryIQw7KQKLOeRT&X-Amz-Signature=b37c605567ae744b53b7f05a546e4b0fa87de9a14ce8fe0d035b8fea90d1cb6a&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

MHA 会根据其他从库的 binlog 位置，也就是 binlog 的 position，找到包含最新更新的从库，作为备用主库。当然了，如果你使用 g t i d 复制 MHA 也是支持的，这个时候就没有 position 了，对吧？之后去应用差异的 relay log 到其他的从库，从而使得其他从库和备用主库的数据保持一致。这是因为不同的从库它的延迟情况可能是不一样的，所以它会有差异。再后来会去应用从原先主库上保存的Binlog，并把数据恢复到所有的数据节点上。最后把备用主库晋升成为新的主库，并让从库和新主库保持主从关系。如果主库宕机非常彻底，已经没有办法通过 ssh 连接的话，那么就不去做第一步以及第四步，其他的步骤则是一样的。OK。



经过分析，我们可以总结两点一是 MHA 的故障切换主要包括三个过程

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/ede75c8f-af22-401c-aa54-2d2bc9506eda/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RBW2QQVM%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231213Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCICgAwAXbj1gh8jyHKgjjJ%2FLYX2mdCEEEo8716DiTNwK8AiBQfVlY4738ISFpguGSkhKIv4mu%2BAU%2Fy05sOw4YBZ0KzyqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIMf9y6Q3pH7MoB%2BnggKtwDoMndApzs2fqpLlt2EHgT0maf%2FZTFGogO3Hv44KZ1bi2%2Fs5XeAYoXfrcF0gAwketkIC5nNXyIMVNBuvp79pDL0squcyS74h49A3ucqYDqLZVDwzqr3WxG1TdxdetcPzcdH5EtC13j1Zcn7N0kgYKGt7EDyNrJA1LqUsDOnv9%2BZpvqGVNaCSoeJaPhvhgoo4zPst%2FyRSb16czls7pv1Z7pl24e9D4odvzdFrLR0cqtPP8vmobsWwya1W%2BoYd25SCa0iPuzeMdYp5m2u5fKNmKLN%2FCVf7O%2BCNTKua7yCysqCmgEBeoZ8qGnMVGAoTC3Zhbd6Ws3ygc%2F4TTNoDNf5qqSCF7Wtrm3d%2FO3eyfTevWcprM1RLiK5451Bba99HloSouzAbFyPusOMEuQYDx5%2Bs9kMZSMQEN7qXCHrXx3ezODfP0H%2FY7jtyUaBFUF1DMWA%2BMbf9lTUGBVT%2FwWVygxQtOuEIc88spnABaKf1VBZlQYSmFtQRTobTglIGqK4%2BuxaWX8xeKGB%2F4zTi%2BqzgXwN%2BTFrdigohLSI%2BQo6qAcowtXsoiSufIPeD5lgaf22q1ZAKZDISWc1Uk2CqqTyZVDa%2Fy3dz%2BL8X3T8sljdIe61mmeb9Q9%2FnEOEi0rm4X67iMw2rf%2F0gY6pgHpc0v%2FtRxZH%2B9yUignjKSwFTPxF9YYTBXHBCfLrG3FXgC2w4rF4KfYTIQg2yb1r5E9DEmdJiJETR%2BNvRIOSmFWH2A1KfcyDzI8NIFcblFS%2BHz6oJVyl7uj%2FyFB6pNXXCMG1NE0CDUa18dlqZnVYHS8wTIzf8IhVsNHahYxM9yOWRUutrSy62coWyJtL%2Flm6Ya5uDx14H3fT9irNqryIQw7KQKLOeRT&X-Amz-Signature=4d75901a3a90fbf6ea9ee456bc8ce8fa42f982ace55661db7a7595b292bf445a&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

选择新主库、数据补齐、角色切换二是 MLG 在切换的过程中，从库的恢复是依赖 relalog 的，而默认情况下， relay log 会在 SQL read 执行完毕之后就自动删除了。所以建议把 relay log purge 设成off，让 MySQL 不自动清理 relay log，以便于从库的数据恢复。好。这是 MHA 的原理。下面来看一下 MHA 的详细组成。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/0ffd3355-17dd-44c9-912d-0812e12a0907/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RBW2QQVM%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231213Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCICgAwAXbj1gh8jyHKgjjJ%2FLYX2mdCEEEo8716DiTNwK8AiBQfVlY4738ISFpguGSkhKIv4mu%2BAU%2Fy05sOw4YBZ0KzyqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIMf9y6Q3pH7MoB%2BnggKtwDoMndApzs2fqpLlt2EHgT0maf%2FZTFGogO3Hv44KZ1bi2%2Fs5XeAYoXfrcF0gAwketkIC5nNXyIMVNBuvp79pDL0squcyS74h49A3ucqYDqLZVDwzqr3WxG1TdxdetcPzcdH5EtC13j1Zcn7N0kgYKGt7EDyNrJA1LqUsDOnv9%2BZpvqGVNaCSoeJaPhvhgoo4zPst%2FyRSb16czls7pv1Z7pl24e9D4odvzdFrLR0cqtPP8vmobsWwya1W%2BoYd25SCa0iPuzeMdYp5m2u5fKNmKLN%2FCVf7O%2BCNTKua7yCysqCmgEBeoZ8qGnMVGAoTC3Zhbd6Ws3ygc%2F4TTNoDNf5qqSCF7Wtrm3d%2FO3eyfTevWcprM1RLiK5451Bba99HloSouzAbFyPusOMEuQYDx5%2Bs9kMZSMQEN7qXCHrXx3ezODfP0H%2FY7jtyUaBFUF1DMWA%2BMbf9lTUGBVT%2FwWVygxQtOuEIc88spnABaKf1VBZlQYSmFtQRTobTglIGqK4%2BuxaWX8xeKGB%2F4zTi%2BqzgXwN%2BTFrdigohLSI%2BQo6qAcowtXsoiSufIPeD5lgaf22q1ZAKZDISWc1Uk2CqqTyZVDa%2Fy3dz%2BL8X3T8sljdIe61mmeb9Q9%2FnEOEi0rm4X67iMw2rf%2F0gY6pgHpc0v%2FtRxZH%2B9yUignjKSwFTPxF9YYTBXHBCfLrG3FXgC2w4rF4KfYTIQg2yb1r5E9DEmdJiJETR%2BNvRIOSmFWH2A1KfcyDzI8NIFcblFS%2BHz6oJVyl7uj%2FyFB6pNXXCMG1NE0CDUa18dlqZnVYHS8wTIzf8IhVsNHahYxM9yOWRUutrSy62coWyJtL%2Flm6Ya5uDx14H3fT9irNqryIQw7KQKLOeRT&X-Amz-Signature=746bc719c9d900613eeb142e9c3ddb3311df4974a686e67f5b2697f88f343e64&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

前面说过 MHA，它是一个基于脚本的工具。 MHA 由 manager 和 node 组成。下面来看一看到底包含了哪些工具。 MHA manager 里面包含了这几个工具 must check ssh 用来检查 MHA 的 ssh 配置。 masterha check replication 用来检查 MySQL 复制。 masterHA manager 是 MHA 的管理工具。 masterHA check status 用来检测当前 MHA 的运行状态。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/3389b5a0-ac1e-44b2-ba47-9b97dc0e57db/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RBW2QQVM%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231213Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCICgAwAXbj1gh8jyHKgjjJ%2FLYX2mdCEEEo8716DiTNwK8AiBQfVlY4738ISFpguGSkhKIv4mu%2BAU%2Fy05sOw4YBZ0KzyqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIMf9y6Q3pH7MoB%2BnggKtwDoMndApzs2fqpLlt2EHgT0maf%2FZTFGogO3Hv44KZ1bi2%2Fs5XeAYoXfrcF0gAwketkIC5nNXyIMVNBuvp79pDL0squcyS74h49A3ucqYDqLZVDwzqr3WxG1TdxdetcPzcdH5EtC13j1Zcn7N0kgYKGt7EDyNrJA1LqUsDOnv9%2BZpvqGVNaCSoeJaPhvhgoo4zPst%2FyRSb16czls7pv1Z7pl24e9D4odvzdFrLR0cqtPP8vmobsWwya1W%2BoYd25SCa0iPuzeMdYp5m2u5fKNmKLN%2FCVf7O%2BCNTKua7yCysqCmgEBeoZ8qGnMVGAoTC3Zhbd6Ws3ygc%2F4TTNoDNf5qqSCF7Wtrm3d%2FO3eyfTevWcprM1RLiK5451Bba99HloSouzAbFyPusOMEuQYDx5%2Bs9kMZSMQEN7qXCHrXx3ezODfP0H%2FY7jtyUaBFUF1DMWA%2BMbf9lTUGBVT%2FwWVygxQtOuEIc88spnABaKf1VBZlQYSmFtQRTobTglIGqK4%2BuxaWX8xeKGB%2F4zTi%2BqzgXwN%2BTFrdigohLSI%2BQo6qAcowtXsoiSufIPeD5lgaf22q1ZAKZDISWc1Uk2CqqTyZVDa%2Fy3dz%2BL8X3T8sljdIe61mmeb9Q9%2FnEOEi0rm4X67iMw2rf%2F0gY6pgHpc0v%2FtRxZH%2B9yUignjKSwFTPxF9YYTBXHBCfLrG3FXgC2w4rF4KfYTIQg2yb1r5E9DEmdJiJETR%2BNvRIOSmFWH2A1KfcyDzI8NIFcblFS%2BHz6oJVyl7uj%2FyFB6pNXXCMG1NE0CDUa18dlqZnVYHS8wTIzf8IhVsNHahYxM9yOWRUutrSy62coWyJtL%2Flm6Ya5uDx14H3fT9irNqryIQw7KQKLOeRT&X-Amz-Signature=1d459a74285af63b03c201e057b970f9face00d37585cf4e35f06920f0ea85d8&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

masterha master monitor 用来监控 MySQL 主节点的状态，比方监控是不是宕机。 masterha must switch 用来控制故障转移，可以自动控制，也可以去手动控制。 must HA CONF host，用来添加或者删除配置的主机信息，这是 MHA manager。


再来看 MHA node。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/a8ce7793-e858-4796-9ed4-242b47a8d02a/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RBW2QQVM%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231213Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCICgAwAXbj1gh8jyHKgjjJ%2FLYX2mdCEEEo8716DiTNwK8AiBQfVlY4738ISFpguGSkhKIv4mu%2BAU%2Fy05sOw4YBZ0KzyqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIMf9y6Q3pH7MoB%2BnggKtwDoMndApzs2fqpLlt2EHgT0maf%2FZTFGogO3Hv44KZ1bi2%2Fs5XeAYoXfrcF0gAwketkIC5nNXyIMVNBuvp79pDL0squcyS74h49A3ucqYDqLZVDwzqr3WxG1TdxdetcPzcdH5EtC13j1Zcn7N0kgYKGt7EDyNrJA1LqUsDOnv9%2BZpvqGVNaCSoeJaPhvhgoo4zPst%2FyRSb16czls7pv1Z7pl24e9D4odvzdFrLR0cqtPP8vmobsWwya1W%2BoYd25SCa0iPuzeMdYp5m2u5fKNmKLN%2FCVf7O%2BCNTKua7yCysqCmgEBeoZ8qGnMVGAoTC3Zhbd6Ws3ygc%2F4TTNoDNf5qqSCF7Wtrm3d%2FO3eyfTevWcprM1RLiK5451Bba99HloSouzAbFyPusOMEuQYDx5%2Bs9kMZSMQEN7qXCHrXx3ezODfP0H%2FY7jtyUaBFUF1DMWA%2BMbf9lTUGBVT%2FwWVygxQtOuEIc88spnABaKf1VBZlQYSmFtQRTobTglIGqK4%2BuxaWX8xeKGB%2F4zTi%2BqzgXwN%2BTFrdigohLSI%2BQo6qAcowtXsoiSufIPeD5lgaf22q1ZAKZDISWc1Uk2CqqTyZVDa%2Fy3dz%2BL8X3T8sljdIe61mmeb9Q9%2FnEOEi0rm4X67iMw2rf%2F0gY6pgHpc0v%2FtRxZH%2B9yUignjKSwFTPxF9YYTBXHBCfLrG3FXgC2w4rF4KfYTIQg2yb1r5E9DEmdJiJETR%2BNvRIOSmFWH2A1KfcyDzI8NIFcblFS%2BHz6oJVyl7uj%2FyFB6pNXXCMG1NE0CDUa18dlqZnVYHS8wTIzf8IhVsNHahYxM9yOWRUutrSy62coWyJtL%2Flm6Ya5uDx14H3fT9irNqryIQw7KQKLOeRT&X-Amz-Signature=71ad560743ec9626e7f34c58c06aa577a8750349a71eb2bccc04a3140c78c234&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

 MHA node 包含了这么几个工具一是 save binary logs，用了保存和复制主节点的binlog。二是 apply diff relay logs，用来识别差异的 relay log 事件，并应用于其他从节点。说白了，对比其他从节点和备用节点的差异。三是 purge relay logs，用来清除 relay log。前面我们不是说了嘛，要关闭掉MySQL，自动清理 relay log，所以可以使用这个工具去清理relog。


当然了， MHA node 里面的这些工具一般都是由 MHA manager 的脚本去触发的，而不需要人工操作。下面来不选买垂。


这里我准备了 4 台全新安装的服务器，

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/f32bf8b4-cb0c-4fca-8e8a-f0909399b3a1/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RBW2QQVM%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231213Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCICgAwAXbj1gh8jyHKgjjJ%2FLYX2mdCEEEo8716DiTNwK8AiBQfVlY4738ISFpguGSkhKIv4mu%2BAU%2Fy05sOw4YBZ0KzyqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIMf9y6Q3pH7MoB%2BnggKtwDoMndApzs2fqpLlt2EHgT0maf%2FZTFGogO3Hv44KZ1bi2%2Fs5XeAYoXfrcF0gAwketkIC5nNXyIMVNBuvp79pDL0squcyS74h49A3ucqYDqLZVDwzqr3WxG1TdxdetcPzcdH5EtC13j1Zcn7N0kgYKGt7EDyNrJA1LqUsDOnv9%2BZpvqGVNaCSoeJaPhvhgoo4zPst%2FyRSb16czls7pv1Z7pl24e9D4odvzdFrLR0cqtPP8vmobsWwya1W%2BoYd25SCa0iPuzeMdYp5m2u5fKNmKLN%2FCVf7O%2BCNTKua7yCysqCmgEBeoZ8qGnMVGAoTC3Zhbd6Ws3ygc%2F4TTNoDNf5qqSCF7Wtrm3d%2FO3eyfTevWcprM1RLiK5451Bba99HloSouzAbFyPusOMEuQYDx5%2Bs9kMZSMQEN7qXCHrXx3ezODfP0H%2FY7jtyUaBFUF1DMWA%2BMbf9lTUGBVT%2FwWVygxQtOuEIc88spnABaKf1VBZlQYSmFtQRTobTglIGqK4%2BuxaWX8xeKGB%2F4zTi%2BqzgXwN%2BTFrdigohLSI%2BQo6qAcowtXsoiSufIPeD5lgaf22q1ZAKZDISWc1Uk2CqqTyZVDa%2Fy3dz%2BL8X3T8sljdIe61mmeb9Q9%2FnEOEi0rm4X67iMw2rf%2F0gY6pgHpc0v%2FtRxZH%2B9yUignjKSwFTPxF9YYTBXHBCfLrG3FXgC2w4rF4KfYTIQg2yb1r5E9DEmdJiJETR%2BNvRIOSmFWH2A1KfcyDzI8NIFcblFS%2BHz6oJVyl7uj%2FyFB6pNXXCMG1NE0CDUa18dlqZnVYHS8wTIzf8IhVsNHahYxM9yOWRUutrSy62coWyJtL%2Flm6Ya5uDx14H3fT9irNqryIQw7KQKLOeRT&X-Amz-Signature=c1d9bb6249055380be55ab6e22e724d9ed234108904b5150099acbbc049bcb6e&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

包括一个主节点，两个从节点以及一个 MHA manager。当然了，每台机器上面都需要安装 MHA node。另外 slave master 这台机器会在 master 这台机器挂掉之后成为新的主节点。


好，下面来过一下这个文档。


首先在 3 台 MySQL 机器，也就是这 3 台机器安装MySQL。我们来对照这篇文章安装一下。首先下载 MySQL 的 yum 源， copy 一台机器，下载第二台机器，第三台，安装 MySQL 的样元。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/23fe42d5-bfbd-466f-b005-70a53d0579b4/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RBW2QQVM%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231213Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCICgAwAXbj1gh8jyHKgjjJ%2FLYX2mdCEEEo8716DiTNwK8AiBQfVlY4738ISFpguGSkhKIv4mu%2BAU%2Fy05sOw4YBZ0KzyqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIMf9y6Q3pH7MoB%2BnggKtwDoMndApzs2fqpLlt2EHgT0maf%2FZTFGogO3Hv44KZ1bi2%2Fs5XeAYoXfrcF0gAwketkIC5nNXyIMVNBuvp79pDL0squcyS74h49A3ucqYDqLZVDwzqr3WxG1TdxdetcPzcdH5EtC13j1Zcn7N0kgYKGt7EDyNrJA1LqUsDOnv9%2BZpvqGVNaCSoeJaPhvhgoo4zPst%2FyRSb16czls7pv1Z7pl24e9D4odvzdFrLR0cqtPP8vmobsWwya1W%2BoYd25SCa0iPuzeMdYp5m2u5fKNmKLN%2FCVf7O%2BCNTKua7yCysqCmgEBeoZ8qGnMVGAoTC3Zhbd6Ws3ygc%2F4TTNoDNf5qqSCF7Wtrm3d%2FO3eyfTevWcprM1RLiK5451Bba99HloSouzAbFyPusOMEuQYDx5%2Bs9kMZSMQEN7qXCHrXx3ezODfP0H%2FY7jtyUaBFUF1DMWA%2BMbf9lTUGBVT%2FwWVygxQtOuEIc88spnABaKf1VBZlQYSmFtQRTobTglIGqK4%2BuxaWX8xeKGB%2F4zTi%2BqzgXwN%2BTFrdigohLSI%2BQo6qAcowtXsoiSufIPeD5lgaf22q1ZAKZDISWc1Uk2CqqTyZVDa%2Fy3dz%2BL8X3T8sljdIe61mmeb9Q9%2FnEOEi0rm4X67iMw2rf%2F0gY6pgHpc0v%2FtRxZH%2B9yUignjKSwFTPxF9YYTBXHBCfLrG3FXgC2w4rF4KfYTIQg2yb1r5E9DEmdJiJETR%2BNvRIOSmFWH2A1KfcyDzI8NIFcblFS%2BHz6oJVyl7uj%2FyFB6pNXXCMG1NE0CDUa18dlqZnVYHS8wTIzf8IhVsNHahYxM9yOWRUutrSy62coWyJtL%2Flm6Ya5uDx14H3fT9irNqryIQw7KQKLOeRT&X-Amz-Signature=a64e67ff06e7e87fe84676f752fc21dabac4ea6fe010e4ad5ff720bc35295139&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

安装。接着安装MySQL。

安装需要一段时间，我们稍等一下。


接着启动MySQL。启动，启动， 启动， 可以使用 systemctl status mysqld.service 去查看 MySQL 的服务状态，我们这里就不查了。理论上启动没有报错，启动就是成功的。

根据使用 grep 去查看初始密码。执行。执行。连接MySQL，注入出行密码，重置密码。默认情况下， MySQL 的密码安全要求比较高，所以设置这样的密码会报错。我们需要先设置一个安全性比较高的密码，执行。第二台，第三台。如果你想设置低安全性的密码，需要执行一下这两行命令，我们也执行一下。执行事情， copy 执行,  执行，就行。之后，就可以 设置第一安全性的密码了。我个人对 root123 这样的密码是情有独钟。粘贴，粘贴好，密码重置完成。最后允许 root 用户远程连接粘贴。这里把 host 设成百分号，意思是允许入的用户从任何地方连接。


最后 flash 一下，授权。好 MySQL 安装完毕。之后开放 3306 以及 22 端口。或者是关闭防火墙。当然了，生产环境不太建议。由于我是阿里云上购买的机器，所以防火墙默认关闭的。这一步我们可以跳过。此外还要关闭 SELinux，对于阿里云上的机器默认也是关闭的，所以我们也可以跳过。


OK，下面来配置，主动复制。稍微的复习一下前面的内容。

首先编辑 MySQL 配置文件， exit 编辑 ， exit  然后拷贝配置，进入编辑模式粘贴。从中可以发现，我们的主从复制是基于GTID 的。这些参数前面都详细讲过了。除此以外，我们还设了一个 relay log purge off，让 MySQL 无去自动清零。 relay log 好保存。修改第二台机器 i 粘贴，修改 server ID，把它改成比如 2 OK 修改第三代机器，I，粘贴，修改server_id  =3 , OK。最后，重启MySQL，到主节点创建用户，用来实现主从复制芭比 MySQL  -uroot  -proot123。



看清楚，为 repl 用户授予 replication slave 权限，粘贴， flush 刷新授权到两台从接点执行 changing master。配置主从 copy，第一代从节点就行。第二点从节点，已经。由于我们是基于 g t i d 复制的，所以不需要知道 binlog 的文件名称以及position。接着执行 start slave，开启主从复制。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/f9ba1e79-fb13-40eb-aca7-3c61472867f4/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RBW2QQVM%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231214Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCICgAwAXbj1gh8jyHKgjjJ%2FLYX2mdCEEEo8716DiTNwK8AiBQfVlY4738ISFpguGSkhKIv4mu%2BAU%2Fy05sOw4YBZ0KzyqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIMf9y6Q3pH7MoB%2BnggKtwDoMndApzs2fqpLlt2EHgT0maf%2FZTFGogO3Hv44KZ1bi2%2Fs5XeAYoXfrcF0gAwketkIC5nNXyIMVNBuvp79pDL0squcyS74h49A3ucqYDqLZVDwzqr3WxG1TdxdetcPzcdH5EtC13j1Zcn7N0kgYKGt7EDyNrJA1LqUsDOnv9%2BZpvqGVNaCSoeJaPhvhgoo4zPst%2FyRSb16czls7pv1Z7pl24e9D4odvzdFrLR0cqtPP8vmobsWwya1W%2BoYd25SCa0iPuzeMdYp5m2u5fKNmKLN%2FCVf7O%2BCNTKua7yCysqCmgEBeoZ8qGnMVGAoTC3Zhbd6Ws3ygc%2F4TTNoDNf5qqSCF7Wtrm3d%2FO3eyfTevWcprM1RLiK5451Bba99HloSouzAbFyPusOMEuQYDx5%2Bs9kMZSMQEN7qXCHrXx3ezODfP0H%2FY7jtyUaBFUF1DMWA%2BMbf9lTUGBVT%2FwWVygxQtOuEIc88spnABaKf1VBZlQYSmFtQRTobTglIGqK4%2BuxaWX8xeKGB%2F4zTi%2BqzgXwN%2BTFrdigohLSI%2BQo6qAcowtXsoiSufIPeD5lgaf22q1ZAKZDISWc1Uk2CqqTyZVDa%2Fy3dz%2BL8X3T8sljdIe61mmeb9Q9%2FnEOEi0rm4X67iMw2rf%2F0gY6pgHpc0v%2FtRxZH%2B9yUignjKSwFTPxF9YYTBXHBCfLrG3FXgC2w4rF4KfYTIQg2yb1r5E9DEmdJiJETR%2BNvRIOSmFWH2A1KfcyDzI8NIFcblFS%2BHz6oJVyl7uj%2FyFB6pNXXCMG1NE0CDUa18dlqZnVYHS8wTIzf8IhVsNHahYxM9yOWRUutrSy62coWyJtL%2Flm6Ya5uDx14H3fT9irNqryIQw7KQKLOeRT&X-Amz-Signature=d0c447ac863c3818de638e43edf57cdf2b02a6dd7c2f4212bd18524246ea110e&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

到两台重接点，执行 select user host from MySQL user，看一下有没有 repl 用户。如果有，说明主从复制是成功的，因为我们只在主节点创建了用户对吧。第二个从节点也执行下芭比粘贴没有问题。可以发现这里的主从复制比前面的 g t i d 复制要简单很多。还记得前面我们在配置 g t i d 复制的时候，需要先把 enforce  gtid consistency 设成one，

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/76491bac-5f3a-4b3c-815d-10a42ad455bf/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466RBW2QQVM%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231214Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJGMEQCICgAwAXbj1gh8jyHKgjjJ%2FLYX2mdCEEEo8716DiTNwK8AiBQfVlY4738ISFpguGSkhKIv4mu%2BAU%2Fy05sOw4YBZ0KzyqIBAjG%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F8BEAAaDDYzNzQyMzE4MzgwNSIMf9y6Q3pH7MoB%2BnggKtwDoMndApzs2fqpLlt2EHgT0maf%2FZTFGogO3Hv44KZ1bi2%2Fs5XeAYoXfrcF0gAwketkIC5nNXyIMVNBuvp79pDL0squcyS74h49A3ucqYDqLZVDwzqr3WxG1TdxdetcPzcdH5EtC13j1Zcn7N0kgYKGt7EDyNrJA1LqUsDOnv9%2BZpvqGVNaCSoeJaPhvhgoo4zPst%2FyRSb16czls7pv1Z7pl24e9D4odvzdFrLR0cqtPP8vmobsWwya1W%2BoYd25SCa0iPuzeMdYp5m2u5fKNmKLN%2FCVf7O%2BCNTKua7yCysqCmgEBeoZ8qGnMVGAoTC3Zhbd6Ws3ygc%2F4TTNoDNf5qqSCF7Wtrm3d%2FO3eyfTevWcprM1RLiK5451Bba99HloSouzAbFyPusOMEuQYDx5%2Bs9kMZSMQEN7qXCHrXx3ezODfP0H%2FY7jtyUaBFUF1DMWA%2BMbf9lTUGBVT%2FwWVygxQtOuEIc88spnABaKf1VBZlQYSmFtQRTobTglIGqK4%2BuxaWX8xeKGB%2F4zTi%2BqzgXwN%2BTFrdigohLSI%2BQo6qAcowtXsoiSufIPeD5lgaf22q1ZAKZDISWc1Uk2CqqTyZVDa%2Fy3dz%2BL8X3T8sljdIe61mmeb9Q9%2FnEOEi0rm4X67iMw2rf%2F0gY6pgHpc0v%2FtRxZH%2B9yUignjKSwFTPxF9YYTBXHBCfLrG3FXgC2w4rF4KfYTIQg2yb1r5E9DEmdJiJETR%2BNvRIOSmFWH2A1KfcyDzI8NIFcblFS%2BHz6oJVyl7uj%2FyFB6pNXXCMG1NE0CDUa18dlqZnVYHS8wTIzf8IhVsNHahYxM9yOWRUutrSy62coWyJtL%2Flm6Ya5uDx14H3fT9irNqryIQw7KQKLOeRT&X-Amz-Signature=e5f00613cff456df1c8ac75ab7b0dbd2c56368e0cacc53ec51bd6098545a1ded&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

然后运行一段时间，看错误日志里面有没有警告，如果有警告，还要修改。应用。之后才能把 enforce gtid consistency 设置on。另外，前面我们还要设置 g t i d mod。接着 e mode 默认是off，我们需要把它从 off 变成 off permissive 再变成 on permissive，最后才能变成on。而这里我们是直接把它设成 on 的。这是因为我们是全新安装的MySQL，在配置主从复制之前没有产生Binlog，所以我们把设置这两个参数的过程给省略了。


OK，主从复制配置完成之后来配置虚拟IP。有关什么是虚拟IP，同学们可以参考这篇文章。

[https://www.jianshu.com/p/00660a56cc2c](https://www.jianshu.com/p/00660a56cc2c)

。

最后点击监听配置向导，选择 tcp 端口，输入3306，也就是你的 MySQL 端口监听名称，比如 MHA MySQL 3306。下一步，选择主备服务器组，新建一个主备服务器组，填入名称，比如 MHA MySQL、 master slave

下一步

配置 MySQL 的主节点作为主机，备用主节点则是备机。这样 slb 它会自动监听主机节点的 3306 端口，如果发现不正常就会切到备机。

等下一步，

提交，配置

完成。


这里有一个bug，我们需要人工的跳转一下，点击展开完成。效果是这样的这样当我们访问虚拟 IP 的时候，在主节点正常的时候会跳到主节点，主节点不正常的时候会跳到备用主节点。好配置完成

，之后在主节点执行 if config， exit 获得网卡名称 ETH 0，

然后，执行 /sbin/ifconfig  eth0  跟上网卡名称冒号，一再跟上 SLB 的虚拟 IP 执行。再次执行一次 ifconfig。可以看到训练 IP 已经配置 OK 了。

首先在每台机器执行 ssh-keygen 生成密钥，一台机器执行回车，第二台机器执行回车，第三台机器，第四台继续。

首先在主节点创建一个用户，这个用户是给 MHA 去使用的。主节点登录，

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/d3409f22-9c0c-49fb-9bcb-85408f5d66c9/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466ZN2MZQJJ%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231214Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIGAZSgHHnWANzA7WgOE6mR7l7nbnNGP%2BzWXMjzY3EHwxAiEArp6tKmYUpfbMnEQGXPA5NVMzDo7CinJAs44zBB1sXzAqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDK%2B%2FXpIgfy5BmaGWzyrcA60bTHm1T%2BuVKFu5FYCVREp6roilDjZLh2Nv%2FiU8oX5f8rqwe2eBIW9uk3DlznHDP%2Bpz5pVCdIRhNKXozTd0UTAjQk%2BprfKroK0wNK%2B5ph%2BGcWCaUgC0zg9hYvXdHEAewaEb9dmBg9dyUtsgtpUZlwSg%2FLrsdLz7GDshqwrpv7DS8gj9iKQLpaSkcThsHh%2FFLM13IYNoNTGONI67xuxJU91rvAFnyMwCyRGB%2FUGxvSze07YCnvyZoTanlLuU5MRP03zlq%2FEXdiAPn5Ggwkzer%2FC8Fj13uS1yUjW6ACF9Zdy7cw76E%2FXVK3QpV8wEAIGeN%2BM2tePRJmiXiaEW%2BYtSxMNehB5n%2BVvzve5qEZENUexwv1LSBUcZ3gNLuUCdAkCGmtwORz%2BvoNALU%2BIyQnyhZcj1TVbt3h682dTN7yS46k1ubfUsmgXOslShqZT2x5Wg7zkQdchPD5H7K2iHMdl8dZMm2%2FGgNr9V6QnK3n5dYUkYSUV1z1tlyqPaJfHCM8JlbeNZq%2B8%2FLTLfWsD3nwC8AQt3f1IRfcbIsduvSmsCcfTGELKrUikPTKz31GzyBt%2FaGHltIMdzonUwwMTnBiXiuZ%2Bfnn93DnQ2Iwe7zrtEiGnXyst9EbUJt65MoBmPMJq6%2F9IGOqUBM6zC8C7KiIBss%2BlxNmA96H%2BPNijkL47Iau3C5CMXM3BoRVSrM7T%2FCeWkMxRweKbw7aQ60mkxFctPO8MbHm6vUQWHu94I4L1E5EKne7b9%2BPWCmloST8dGLmml8tzpzhR4Xxfpi%2BTqefbEi5zThdNYf%2Bi12bo18DwCFj%2FTBIEqQWhrpb%2B%2F%2BitR0bHaPf%2FOr%2FS2b%2Fyyl4ODkicGpzEbOoCKPe6zfswo&X-Amz-Signature=960a77e7e13811c89924c69cac271494403e63526d0846ec65e05a169a5ba4f1&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

创建，给用户授予 all privileges。大家可以发现 MHA 所使用的是 all  villages，而前面主从复制的用户 i p 2 使用的则是 replication slave。一定要注意一下， flash 刷新授权。


在每一台机器安装 EPLE 源 。这里，一台机器安装第二条，第三台，第四。如果安装速度比较慢，也可以用这种方式去安装。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/75dd17c2-8e74-4fdb-8e0e-5adbdd22af88/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466ZN2MZQJJ%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231214Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIGAZSgHHnWANzA7WgOE6mR7l7nbnNGP%2BzWXMjzY3EHwxAiEArp6tKmYUpfbMnEQGXPA5NVMzDo7CinJAs44zBB1sXzAqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDK%2B%2FXpIgfy5BmaGWzyrcA60bTHm1T%2BuVKFu5FYCVREp6roilDjZLh2Nv%2FiU8oX5f8rqwe2eBIW9uk3DlznHDP%2Bpz5pVCdIRhNKXozTd0UTAjQk%2BprfKroK0wNK%2B5ph%2BGcWCaUgC0zg9hYvXdHEAewaEb9dmBg9dyUtsgtpUZlwSg%2FLrsdLz7GDshqwrpv7DS8gj9iKQLpaSkcThsHh%2FFLM13IYNoNTGONI67xuxJU91rvAFnyMwCyRGB%2FUGxvSze07YCnvyZoTanlLuU5MRP03zlq%2FEXdiAPn5Ggwkzer%2FC8Fj13uS1yUjW6ACF9Zdy7cw76E%2FXVK3QpV8wEAIGeN%2BM2tePRJmiXiaEW%2BYtSxMNehB5n%2BVvzve5qEZENUexwv1LSBUcZ3gNLuUCdAkCGmtwORz%2BvoNALU%2BIyQnyhZcj1TVbt3h682dTN7yS46k1ubfUsmgXOslShqZT2x5Wg7zkQdchPD5H7K2iHMdl8dZMm2%2FGgNr9V6QnK3n5dYUkYSUV1z1tlyqPaJfHCM8JlbeNZq%2B8%2FLTLfWsD3nwC8AQt3f1IRfcbIsduvSmsCcfTGELKrUikPTKz31GzyBt%2FaGHltIMdzonUwwMTnBiXiuZ%2Bfnn93DnQ2Iwe7zrtEiGnXyst9EbUJt65MoBmPMJq6%2F9IGOqUBM6zC8C7KiIBss%2BlxNmA96H%2BPNijkL47Iau3C5CMXM3BoRVSrM7T%2FCeWkMxRweKbw7aQ60mkxFctPO8MbHm6vUQWHu94I4L1E5EKne7b9%2BPWCmloST8dGLmml8tzpzhR4Xxfpi%2BTqefbEi5zThdNYf%2Bi12bo18DwCFj%2FTBIEqQWhrpb%2B%2F%2BitR0bHaPf%2FOr%2FS2b%2Fyyl4ODkicGpzEbOoCKPe6zfswo&X-Amz-Signature=a08ef537360b32f5954c752f6044db5679585c279b425b7b984af109a8712ee9&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

在每一台机器安装 perl 相关的包，这些包是 MHA node 需要用的

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/d4beec30-f603-4bf4-9363-8f363a85d405/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466ZN2MZQJJ%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231214Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIGAZSgHHnWANzA7WgOE6mR7l7nbnNGP%2BzWXMjzY3EHwxAiEArp6tKmYUpfbMnEQGXPA5NVMzDo7CinJAs44zBB1sXzAqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDK%2B%2FXpIgfy5BmaGWzyrcA60bTHm1T%2BuVKFu5FYCVREp6roilDjZLh2Nv%2FiU8oX5f8rqwe2eBIW9uk3DlznHDP%2Bpz5pVCdIRhNKXozTd0UTAjQk%2BprfKroK0wNK%2B5ph%2BGcWCaUgC0zg9hYvXdHEAewaEb9dmBg9dyUtsgtpUZlwSg%2FLrsdLz7GDshqwrpv7DS8gj9iKQLpaSkcThsHh%2FFLM13IYNoNTGONI67xuxJU91rvAFnyMwCyRGB%2FUGxvSze07YCnvyZoTanlLuU5MRP03zlq%2FEXdiAPn5Ggwkzer%2FC8Fj13uS1yUjW6ACF9Zdy7cw76E%2FXVK3QpV8wEAIGeN%2BM2tePRJmiXiaEW%2BYtSxMNehB5n%2BVvzve5qEZENUexwv1LSBUcZ3gNLuUCdAkCGmtwORz%2BvoNALU%2BIyQnyhZcj1TVbt3h682dTN7yS46k1ubfUsmgXOslShqZT2x5Wg7zkQdchPD5H7K2iHMdl8dZMm2%2FGgNr9V6QnK3n5dYUkYSUV1z1tlyqPaJfHCM8JlbeNZq%2B8%2FLTLfWsD3nwC8AQt3f1IRfcbIsduvSmsCcfTGELKrUikPTKz31GzyBt%2FaGHltIMdzonUwwMTnBiXiuZ%2Bfnn93DnQ2Iwe7zrtEiGnXyst9EbUJt65MoBmPMJq6%2F9IGOqUBM6zC8C7KiIBss%2BlxNmA96H%2BPNijkL47Iau3C5CMXM3BoRVSrM7T%2FCeWkMxRweKbw7aQ60mkxFctPO8MbHm6vUQWHu94I4L1E5EKne7b9%2BPWCmloST8dGLmml8tzpzhR4Xxfpi%2BTqefbEi5zThdNYf%2Bi12bo18DwCFj%2FTBIEqQWhrpb%2B%2F%2BitR0bHaPf%2FOr%2FS2b%2Fyyl4ODkicGpzEbOoCKPe6zfswo&X-Amz-Signature=1ac81a0e05bc1eebc99d9539dc8f50bd0858f927aa3728ab799e33cd4c2a93fc&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

一台第二台， 3 台， 4 台。接着下载 MHA node，安装 MHA node 安装完成第二台，第三台第四条。注意 MHA manager 也需要安装 MHA node，否则的话后面安装 MHA manager 包的时候会报错。之后到 MHA manager 机器去, 安装 MHA manager 需要的包也是 perl 相关的一些包了，执行。接着下载 MHA manager，再选中安装完成。

 i 粘贴保存。简单介绍一下这些配置。首先 user 和 password 指的是 MHA 连接数据库的账号和密码，对应的是我们刚刚创建的这个

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/d0918f63-b298-44b8-93f0-d3e85a5b5e4a/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466ZN2MZQJJ%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231215Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIGAZSgHHnWANzA7WgOE6mR7l7nbnNGP%2BzWXMjzY3EHwxAiEArp6tKmYUpfbMnEQGXPA5NVMzDo7CinJAs44zBB1sXzAqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDK%2B%2FXpIgfy5BmaGWzyrcA60bTHm1T%2BuVKFu5FYCVREp6roilDjZLh2Nv%2FiU8oX5f8rqwe2eBIW9uk3DlznHDP%2Bpz5pVCdIRhNKXozTd0UTAjQk%2BprfKroK0wNK%2B5ph%2BGcWCaUgC0zg9hYvXdHEAewaEb9dmBg9dyUtsgtpUZlwSg%2FLrsdLz7GDshqwrpv7DS8gj9iKQLpaSkcThsHh%2FFLM13IYNoNTGONI67xuxJU91rvAFnyMwCyRGB%2FUGxvSze07YCnvyZoTanlLuU5MRP03zlq%2FEXdiAPn5Ggwkzer%2FC8Fj13uS1yUjW6ACF9Zdy7cw76E%2FXVK3QpV8wEAIGeN%2BM2tePRJmiXiaEW%2BYtSxMNehB5n%2BVvzve5qEZENUexwv1LSBUcZ3gNLuUCdAkCGmtwORz%2BvoNALU%2BIyQnyhZcj1TVbt3h682dTN7yS46k1ubfUsmgXOslShqZT2x5Wg7zkQdchPD5H7K2iHMdl8dZMm2%2FGgNr9V6QnK3n5dYUkYSUV1z1tlyqPaJfHCM8JlbeNZq%2B8%2FLTLfWsD3nwC8AQt3f1IRfcbIsduvSmsCcfTGELKrUikPTKz31GzyBt%2FaGHltIMdzonUwwMTnBiXiuZ%2Bfnn93DnQ2Iwe7zrtEiGnXyst9EbUJt65MoBmPMJq6%2F9IGOqUBM6zC8C7KiIBss%2BlxNmA96H%2BPNijkL47Iau3C5CMXM3BoRVSrM7T%2FCeWkMxRweKbw7aQ60mkxFctPO8MbHm6vUQWHu94I4L1E5EKne7b9%2BPWCmloST8dGLmml8tzpzhR4Xxfpi%2BTqefbEi5zThdNYf%2Bi12bo18DwCFj%2FTBIEqQWhrpb%2B%2F%2BitR0bHaPf%2FOr%2FS2b%2Fyyl4ODkicGpzEbOoCKPe6zfswo&X-Amz-Signature=5ef376f15fb37ad6908970cd64524bcf6f639c9c8e0badc00ecd975e12f64a83&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

用户。


manager_workdir 指的是 MHA 的工作目录。 manager_log 指的是 MHA manager 的日志路径。 remote_work_dir 是除 MHA manager 以外的其他机器的 MHA 的功能目录。也就是假设这台机器创建的是 MySQL MHA remote，这里也需要指定成 MySQL MHA remote。 SSH user 指的是我们刚刚配置的 SSH 免密登录的用户。 repl user 以及 repl password 指的是主从复制的账号和密码，对应的是这里的账号和密码，不要搞混。 ping interval 指的是多久检测一下 master 挂掉了，单位是秒， master binlog dir 点是主节点的 binlog 存放目录。


master ip failover script 是当检测到主节点挂掉之后会执行的脚本，用来实现故障转移。 

master ip online change script 用来实现在线切换主从 

secondary check script 用来指定用于二次检查主节点状态的节点。这是什么意思？举个例子，比方，现在我的 manager 认为 master 挂了，但是事实上 master 可能并没有挂，而是 master 和 MHA manager 之间的网络断了。**所以 MHA 它搞了一个二次校验的设计**，它可以让两个或者更多的节点去检查主节点有没有挂。 OK 下面的 server 1,server 2、 server 3 则是 MySQL 的节点。其中 candidate master 表示这个节点可以参与主节点的选举， no master 表示这个节点不参与主节点选举。

接着创建上面需要的 master ip failover script 的脚本，用来实现故障转移。

OK 除此以外，再去创建一个 master ip online change 脚本，用来实现在线主动切换。

i 进入编辑模式。


 copy，粘贴，OK。需要注意的是，虚拟 IP 要根据你的情况修改网卡名称，根据情况修改。 SSH user 要和 SSH 免密登陆所使用的账号保持一致。新旧主节点的密码要和 MHA 用户的密码保持一致。这里的密码设置有点问题，应该改成12345，我们重新 vim 一下。


接着为两个脚本添加可执行权限。

前面我们已经人工检查，主动复制是 OK 的，这里再用脚本检查看看，可以发现也是 OK 的。


最后启动 MHA，启动完成。下面我们来用虚拟 IP 去连接数据库。


比方现在我们在 slave 这台机器执行，链接，连接上了，然后执行。比如 create database test; use test; create table test_sha (id int primary key auto_increment， name varchar(64) ，

好，接着在主节点执行 shutdown 去模拟主节点宕机，等待级表示。之后来到 master slave 节点，执行 ifconfig，可以看到虚拟 IP 已经漂移到这台机器了。


下面再来演示一下主库恢复。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/a16711c4-fc93-45c9-99a7-9ee7a7bdb2d9/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB466ZN2MZQJJ%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231216Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIGAZSgHHnWANzA7WgOE6mR7l7nbnNGP%2BzWXMjzY3EHwxAiEArp6tKmYUpfbMnEQGXPA5NVMzDo7CinJAs44zBB1sXzAqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDK%2B%2FXpIgfy5BmaGWzyrcA60bTHm1T%2BuVKFu5FYCVREp6roilDjZLh2Nv%2FiU8oX5f8rqwe2eBIW9uk3DlznHDP%2Bpz5pVCdIRhNKXozTd0UTAjQk%2BprfKroK0wNK%2B5ph%2BGcWCaUgC0zg9hYvXdHEAewaEb9dmBg9dyUtsgtpUZlwSg%2FLrsdLz7GDshqwrpv7DS8gj9iKQLpaSkcThsHh%2FFLM13IYNoNTGONI67xuxJU91rvAFnyMwCyRGB%2FUGxvSze07YCnvyZoTanlLuU5MRP03zlq%2FEXdiAPn5Ggwkzer%2FC8Fj13uS1yUjW6ACF9Zdy7cw76E%2FXVK3QpV8wEAIGeN%2BM2tePRJmiXiaEW%2BYtSxMNehB5n%2BVvzve5qEZENUexwv1LSBUcZ3gNLuUCdAkCGmtwORz%2BvoNALU%2BIyQnyhZcj1TVbt3h682dTN7yS46k1ubfUsmgXOslShqZT2x5Wg7zkQdchPD5H7K2iHMdl8dZMm2%2FGgNr9V6QnK3n5dYUkYSUV1z1tlyqPaJfHCM8JlbeNZq%2B8%2FLTLfWsD3nwC8AQt3f1IRfcbIsduvSmsCcfTGELKrUikPTKz31GzyBt%2FaGHltIMdzonUwwMTnBiXiuZ%2Bfnn93DnQ2Iwe7zrtEiGnXyst9EbUJt65MoBmPMJq6%2F9IGOqUBM6zC8C7KiIBss%2BlxNmA96H%2BPNijkL47Iau3C5CMXM3BoRVSrM7T%2FCeWkMxRweKbw7aQ60mkxFctPO8MbHm6vUQWHu94I4L1E5EKne7b9%2BPWCmloST8dGLmml8tzpzhR4Xxfpi%2BTqefbEi5zThdNYf%2Bi12bo18DwCFj%2FTBIEqQWhrpb%2B%2F%2BitR0bHaPf%2FOr%2FS2b%2Fyyl4ODkicGpzEbOoCKPe6zfswo&X-Amz-Signature=edaf7731a08e28c0432dfc12ce1d996bd807f24ecc4c9f21bcc968e799b45d91&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

需要注意的是，在原先的主库恢复之前，一定要先修改 SLB 的配置。因为现在 MHA 它认为 207 这台机器是主节点， 206 已经挂了，即使 206 恢复之后， MHA 他依然认为 207 是主节点。而对于 SLB 来说，由于刚刚我们配置了 206 是主节点， 207 是倍节点，所以一旦 206 恢复，就会继续访问 206 了。这样我们用虚拟 IP 发问操作的其实是206，而不是207，这样就会有问题。


点击实例管理点击管理。

点击主备服务器组创建，添加一个新的主备服务器组。依然勾选 206207 两台机器，下一步选定端口 3306, 3306 添加。这一次我们选择 207 式主节点，创建，铁人名称207。看见。之后到监听，点击停止监听。


再创建一个新的监听3306，点击停止，点击修改监听配置。下一步，把它关联到207。主备服务器组。下一步提交。知道了，再启动。我们这里exit。

root23，  use test； select * from test_sha 有数据，


到节点3 退出重新进入看一下节点 3 本地有没有数据，如果有，说明 slave 已经能够同步新的主节点的数据。-uroots -proot123 use test select * from test_sha 没有问题。

启动好之后，还是要在这个节点上执行 changing master，让它作为新主节点的从节点。 MySQL -uroots 杠p，粘贴 start sleeve，现在我们又变成了一组两从的架构。


此外，我们还可以到 MHA manager 节点，执行 master check repl 可以看到，在这里他说 207 是主， 206 以及 208 是从。如果我们还想把 206 作为主库怎么办？可以先配置一下 SLB。

yes。当然了，我们并没有去调整 SLB 的配置。修改好了，我们再用 check repl 看一看现在的主节点是谁。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/a93c0064-09ee-40ec-8eca-ba5931b22699/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4663S7HLM3F%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231216Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIFUV5tTaWjUM1OHTVxeEcqowwRa4yzR09iHoa%2FIjTFmhAiEA9ao3cfS3AFtLPAz18OUh3kJMDkhBDryfAow2b2KE1SQqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDDGTZHKpVpHsJcuINCrcA7q31o6LdstlQX6AGJwJWHS295N0ZVtSExzBK4ucFiEKJFYQo84AmU4fZonDBH6sgwsERjlO1lgXfKB4J4OXMmHkltq48eRJOlA%2BMhZ7E1c0oVo924QBcZOQNYBvJGpC93BdRUXwt5%2FpFv8R0cYFeGI70edClaR%2B7chIlez2cHJAPIVUoQ0OOMdi9PL86vETi5iqP1yU8l%2BuPA5wwiFXCGKBi2KhOPOWedFlWh7Aoz7oRR%2FI6ZmO6HfXffsGbvMiUdlo7qSEmuUZv1ixwAeaUuGQEVq3WddjPl2XWkmNeYeTXJUZPw2gJ67M%2Br%2FIT7IRlMtBbri%2B7O0vZ7iwWDA9cRURcmveE%2F6npfXSzchzp9p%2BoNPWVFfuGQ5tvMQlvwOXMk%2FaFZHAWGYSlWcY7pFUqKBCioclEC55K4d9TH2GXkaqbl%2Bu6fM6Jkt%2FQ2SCVHh8tFKmV899%2BMweeG6pwnGXTWWPWjmX47OVmNYfQay7OvdWWBCfz53hK3FPId5TLvdENg9Mk5eYOUAerVSJuDh2zh7oePfjso6RjxG94YJf2gCAKZGC3x5Ktvs1nkZxRctO4Z19bAhAsw%2B0BM5U%2B%2FU083BiXoGsSFQoC9Lz22bdy%2BCzk5m%2B9Rvqss2qI7%2BZMPG6%2F9IGOqUBQ74Ccd0TiT8QFNft9oUIqw3xYccAdD5j9Lhk5wYyfNJwR8F6K3aKzUdJghoavX0cK8yQarWcNNcaRu9espDLREyXblx2z7oSxW3X9y%2FVOakjgEpfaDGkDa9WqNmfqyH7CWuGGH%2F8PNPfpgPx2oJLVlKgOLhBF9MJxRD1HBbcmUdLDY%2BaZgeSbSyAxZ9u%2FpgaqFqvnH7tN47CGcrgzCNqzN3XywZ5&X-Amz-Signature=fa1481a63f099ac8ad8c0a3508bc83422ae98d86cd8d7387bff0798575cdcfd5&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/00135408-aefd-4ee3-ae49-b1d412238492/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4663S7HLM3F%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231216Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIFUV5tTaWjUM1OHTVxeEcqowwRa4yzR09iHoa%2FIjTFmhAiEA9ao3cfS3AFtLPAz18OUh3kJMDkhBDryfAow2b2KE1SQqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDDGTZHKpVpHsJcuINCrcA7q31o6LdstlQX6AGJwJWHS295N0ZVtSExzBK4ucFiEKJFYQo84AmU4fZonDBH6sgwsERjlO1lgXfKB4J4OXMmHkltq48eRJOlA%2BMhZ7E1c0oVo924QBcZOQNYBvJGpC93BdRUXwt5%2FpFv8R0cYFeGI70edClaR%2B7chIlez2cHJAPIVUoQ0OOMdi9PL86vETi5iqP1yU8l%2BuPA5wwiFXCGKBi2KhOPOWedFlWh7Aoz7oRR%2FI6ZmO6HfXffsGbvMiUdlo7qSEmuUZv1ixwAeaUuGQEVq3WddjPl2XWkmNeYeTXJUZPw2gJ67M%2Br%2FIT7IRlMtBbri%2B7O0vZ7iwWDA9cRURcmveE%2F6npfXSzchzp9p%2BoNPWVFfuGQ5tvMQlvwOXMk%2FaFZHAWGYSlWcY7pFUqKBCioclEC55K4d9TH2GXkaqbl%2Bu6fM6Jkt%2FQ2SCVHh8tFKmV899%2BMweeG6pwnGXTWWPWjmX47OVmNYfQay7OvdWWBCfz53hK3FPId5TLvdENg9Mk5eYOUAerVSJuDh2zh7oePfjso6RjxG94YJf2gCAKZGC3x5Ktvs1nkZxRctO4Z19bAhAsw%2B0BM5U%2B%2FU083BiXoGsSFQoC9Lz22bdy%2BCzk5m%2B9Rvqss2qI7%2BZMPG6%2F9IGOqUBQ74Ccd0TiT8QFNft9oUIqw3xYccAdD5j9Lhk5wYyfNJwR8F6K3aKzUdJghoavX0cK8yQarWcNNcaRu9espDLREyXblx2z7oSxW3X9y%2FVOakjgEpfaDGkDa9WqNmfqyH7CWuGGH%2F8PNPfpgPx2oJLVlKgOLhBF9MJxRD1HBbcmUdLDY%2BaZgeSbSyAxZ9u%2FpgaqFqvnH7tN47CGcrgzCNqzN3XywZ5&X-Amz-Signature=781a07b8eeb3abe6f6fc0cf6d509e4d272df46987558260df9ff59cd8ac7ff28&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

可以看到 206 已经变成主节点了。好 回到 ppt。这是 MHA 的搭建。


下面来分析一下 MHA 的优缺点。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/ac8e8d1a-88dd-4927-9b19-efd0f2a8753a/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4663S7HLM3F%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231216Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIFUV5tTaWjUM1OHTVxeEcqowwRa4yzR09iHoa%2FIjTFmhAiEA9ao3cfS3AFtLPAz18OUh3kJMDkhBDryfAow2b2KE1SQqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDDGTZHKpVpHsJcuINCrcA7q31o6LdstlQX6AGJwJWHS295N0ZVtSExzBK4ucFiEKJFYQo84AmU4fZonDBH6sgwsERjlO1lgXfKB4J4OXMmHkltq48eRJOlA%2BMhZ7E1c0oVo924QBcZOQNYBvJGpC93BdRUXwt5%2FpFv8R0cYFeGI70edClaR%2B7chIlez2cHJAPIVUoQ0OOMdi9PL86vETi5iqP1yU8l%2BuPA5wwiFXCGKBi2KhOPOWedFlWh7Aoz7oRR%2FI6ZmO6HfXffsGbvMiUdlo7qSEmuUZv1ixwAeaUuGQEVq3WddjPl2XWkmNeYeTXJUZPw2gJ67M%2Br%2FIT7IRlMtBbri%2B7O0vZ7iwWDA9cRURcmveE%2F6npfXSzchzp9p%2BoNPWVFfuGQ5tvMQlvwOXMk%2FaFZHAWGYSlWcY7pFUqKBCioclEC55K4d9TH2GXkaqbl%2Bu6fM6Jkt%2FQ2SCVHh8tFKmV899%2BMweeG6pwnGXTWWPWjmX47OVmNYfQay7OvdWWBCfz53hK3FPId5TLvdENg9Mk5eYOUAerVSJuDh2zh7oePfjso6RjxG94YJf2gCAKZGC3x5Ktvs1nkZxRctO4Z19bAhAsw%2B0BM5U%2B%2FU083BiXoGsSFQoC9Lz22bdy%2BCzk5m%2B9Rvqss2qI7%2BZMPG6%2F9IGOqUBQ74Ccd0TiT8QFNft9oUIqw3xYccAdD5j9Lhk5wYyfNJwR8F6K3aKzUdJghoavX0cK8yQarWcNNcaRu9espDLREyXblx2z7oSxW3X9y%2FVOakjgEpfaDGkDa9WqNmfqyH7CWuGGH%2F8PNPfpgPx2oJLVlKgOLhBF9MJxRD1HBbcmUdLDY%2BaZgeSbSyAxZ9u%2FpgaqFqvnH7tN47CGcrgzCNqzN3XywZ5&X-Amz-Signature=792a339b9f658ace37f0bc2815087ea926e8fcf630810feae6039c733bef4cb2&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

它的优点主要有这么几个。首先，能够自动监控主节点自动的故障转移，而且故障转移的速度非常的快，能够控制在 30 秒以内。第二，在做故障转移的时候，会最大程度的保持一致性，不容易产生数据丢失。


第三，使用 MHA 对已有的主从复制架构不需要做重大的修改，只需要在原有的主从复制架构基础上额外安装 MHA node 以及 MHA manager 编辑配的 MHA，就 OK 了。第四， MHA manager 可以管理多套主层复制，这样如果有多套主层复制，管理起来就会非常的方便。


再来看一下 MHA 的缺点。

[image](https://prod-files-secure.s3.us-west-2.amazonaws.com/28cd6f37-bc4c-49e6-8d26-8dc351a825af/8b0011e2-9eb2-4113-bf87-2e3bda25cf3d/Untitled.png?X-Amz-Algorithm=AWS4-HMAC-SHA256&X-Amz-Content-Sha256=UNSIGNED-PAYLOAD&X-Amz-Credential=ASIAZI2LB4663S7HLM3F%2F20260721%2Fus-west-2%2Fs3%2Faws4_request&X-Amz-Date=20260721T231216Z&X-Amz-Expires=3600&X-Amz-Security-Token=IQoJb3JpZ2luX2VjEP3%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FwEaCXVzLXdlc3QtMiJHMEUCIFUV5tTaWjUM1OHTVxeEcqowwRa4yzR09iHoa%2FIjTFmhAiEA9ao3cfS3AFtLPAz18OUh3kJMDkhBDryfAow2b2KE1SQqiAQIxv%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2F%2FARAAGgw2Mzc0MjMxODM4MDUiDDGTZHKpVpHsJcuINCrcA7q31o6LdstlQX6AGJwJWHS295N0ZVtSExzBK4ucFiEKJFYQo84AmU4fZonDBH6sgwsERjlO1lgXfKB4J4OXMmHkltq48eRJOlA%2BMhZ7E1c0oVo924QBcZOQNYBvJGpC93BdRUXwt5%2FpFv8R0cYFeGI70edClaR%2B7chIlez2cHJAPIVUoQ0OOMdi9PL86vETi5iqP1yU8l%2BuPA5wwiFXCGKBi2KhOPOWedFlWh7Aoz7oRR%2FI6ZmO6HfXffsGbvMiUdlo7qSEmuUZv1ixwAeaUuGQEVq3WddjPl2XWkmNeYeTXJUZPw2gJ67M%2Br%2FIT7IRlMtBbri%2B7O0vZ7iwWDA9cRURcmveE%2F6npfXSzchzp9p%2BoNPWVFfuGQ5tvMQlvwOXMk%2FaFZHAWGYSlWcY7pFUqKBCioclEC55K4d9TH2GXkaqbl%2Bu6fM6Jkt%2FQ2SCVHh8tFKmV899%2BMweeG6pwnGXTWWPWjmX47OVmNYfQay7OvdWWBCfz53hK3FPId5TLvdENg9Mk5eYOUAerVSJuDh2zh7oePfjso6RjxG94YJf2gCAKZGC3x5Ktvs1nkZxRctO4Z19bAhAsw%2B0BM5U%2B%2FU083BiXoGsSFQoC9Lz22bdy%2BCzk5m%2B9Rvqss2qI7%2BZMPG6%2F9IGOqUBQ74Ccd0TiT8QFNft9oUIqw3xYccAdD5j9Lhk5wYyfNJwR8F6K3aKzUdJghoavX0cK8yQarWcNNcaRu9espDLREyXblx2z7oSxW3X9y%2FVOakjgEpfaDGkDa9WqNmfqyH7CWuGGH%2F8PNPfpgPx2oJLVlKgOLhBF9MJxRD1HBbcmUdLDY%2BaZgeSbSyAxZ9u%2FpgaqFqvnH7tN47CGcrgzCNqzN3XywZ5&X-Amz-Signature=efaebf8eafa2a9bdce97047aa3a1ed78220aa5dd9cd13be2ed7f441f97a51866&X-Amz-SignedHeaders=host&x-amz-checksum-mode=ENABLED&x-id=GetObject)

一是 MHA 的功能一定程度上取决于脚本的完善程度，很多场景下需要去自己完善脚本，这一点相信同学们已经有所体会了。这里的脚本功能强， MHA 的功能就会比较强。反之，如果脚本功能比较的简单， MHA 的功能也比较有限。


第二个缺点是， MHA 自身并不包含 VIP 自动配置的工具，还需要我们借助其他的组件，

比方 keepalived，或者是课上使用的 SLB。

最后简单总结一下，

这节课咱们探讨了 MHA 是什么，提供哪些功能，分析了 MHA 的原理，最后搭建了一套 MHA。好，这节课就到这里，谢谢大家。
